<td colspan="2" style="text-align: center; padding: 0.5em;"><div><div class="floatnone"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mississippi_River_Lock_and_Dam_number_25_large.jpg"><img alt="Mississippi River Lock and Dam number 25 large.jpg" data-file-height="1000" data-file-width="1500" decoding="async" height="187" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Mississippi_River_Lock_and_Dam_number_25_large.jpg/280px-Mississippi_River_Lock_and_Dam_number_25_large.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Mississippi_River_Lock_and_Dam_number_25_large.jpg/420px-Mississippi_River_Lock_and_Dam_number_25_large.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Mississippi_River_Lock_and_Dam_number_25_large.jpg/560px-Mississippi_River_Lock_and_Dam_number_25_large.jpg 2x" width="280"/></a></div></div><div style="padding-top:0.4em"> 流经<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%86%E8%98%87%E9%87%8C%E5%B7%9E" title="密苏里州">密苏里州</a>（左方）与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BC%8A%E5%88%A9%E8%AB%BE%E5%B7%9E" title="伊利诺州">伊利诺州</a>（右方）交界的密西西比河，以及连接两岸的25号闸坝 </div>
</td></tr>
<tr class="mergedtoprow" title="词源（名称起源）">

<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mississippi-map.gif"><img alt="Mississippi-map.gif" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="400" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Mississippi-map.gif/220px-Mississippi-map.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Mississippi-map.gif/330px-Mississippi-map.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/ea/Mississippi-map.gif 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mississippi-map.gif" title="放大"></a></div></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:326px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mississippi_River_map.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="870" data-file-width="1386" decoding="async" height="203" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Mississippi_River_map.png/324px-Mississippi_River_map.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Mississippi_River_map.png/486px-Mississippi_River_map.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/62/Mississippi_River_map.png/648px-Mississippi_River_map.png 2x" width="324"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mississippi_River_map.png" title="放大"></a></div>密西西比河地图</div></div></div>
<p><b>密西西比河</b><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup>（英语：<span lang="en">Mississippi River</span>），位于<a href="/wiki/%E5%8C%97%E7%BE%8E%E6%B4%B2" title="北美洲">北美洲</a>中南部，是北美最大的<a href="/wiki/%E6%B0%B4%E7%B3%BB" title="水系">水系</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-USGSlongest_6-0"><a href="#cite_note-USGSlongest-6">[6]</a></sup>，流域面积约为300万<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E5%85%AC%E9%87%8C" title="平方公里">平方公里</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cws_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-cws-7">[7]</a></sup>。它也是北美最长的河流，源头在<a href="/wiki/%E7%BE%8E%E5%9B%BD" title="美国">美国</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%98%8E%E5%B0%BC%E8%8B%8F%E8%BE%BE%E5%B7%9E" title="明尼苏达州">明尼苏达州</a>西北部海拔446米的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Lake Itasca" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="艾塔斯卡湖"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%89%BE%E5%A1%94%E6%96%AF%E5%8D%A1%E6%B9%96&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="艾塔斯卡湖（页面不存在）">艾塔斯卡湖</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lake_Itasca" title="en:Lake Itasca"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Lake Itasca</span></a></span>）</span></span>（<span lang="en">Lake Itasca</span>），流经<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E5%A4%AE%E5%A4%A7%E5%B9%B3%E5%8E%9F" title="中央大平原">中央大平原</a>，向南注入<a href="/wiki/%E5%A2%A8%E8%A5%BF%E5%93%A5%E6%B9%BE" title="墨西哥湾">墨西哥湾</a>。最长支流<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AF%86%E8%98%87%E9%87%8C%E6%B2%B3" title="密苏里河">密苏里河</a>的源头雷德罗克湖，全长3767公里<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cws_7-1"><a href="#cite_note-cws-7">[7]</a></sup>。如果按照密西西比河的支流——<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%86%E8%8B%8F%E9%87%8C%E6%B2%B3" title="密苏里河">密苏里河</a>的源头计算，则全长为6021公里，居世界河流的第4位<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cws_7-2"><a href="#cite_note-cws-7">[7]</a></sup>，其集水范围可以作为美国中西部的分界。
</p><p>密西西比河的名称源自于美国北部<a href="/wiki/%E5%A8%81%E6%96%AF%E5%BA%B7%E8%BE%9B%E5%B7%9E" title="威斯康辛州">威斯康辛州</a>的印第安阿尔贡金人，因为它支流众多，美国人又尊称为“老人河”，与<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%BC%E7%BD%97%E6%B2%B3" title="尼罗河">尼罗河</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BA%9A%E9%A9%AC%E9%80%8A%E6%B2%B3" title="亚马逊河">亚马逊河</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E9%95%BF%E6%B1%9F" title="长江">长江</a>合称世界四大长河，是北美大陆流域面积最广的水系，两岸多湖泊和沼泽。河流年均输沙量4.95亿吨。流域属世界三大<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%BB%91%E5%9C%9F%E5%8D%80" title="黑土区">黑土区</a>之一。
</p>
<div aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading" class="toc" id="toc" role="navigation"><input class="toctogglecheckbox" id="toctogglecheckbox" role="button" style="display:none" type="checkbox"/><div class="toctitle" dir="ltr" lang="zh"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">目录</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>

<h2><span id=".E6.B0.B4.E6.96.87"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="水文">水文</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：水文">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>密西西比河西边的支流比东边多而长，形成了一大型树枝状水系。水量丰富，近河口的年均流量达1.68万立方米/秒。
</p>
<ul><li>从源头艾塔斯卡湖至<a href="/wiki/%E6%98%8E%E5%B0%BC%E9%98%BF%E6%B3%A2%E5%88%A9%E6%96%AF" title="明尼阿波利斯">明尼阿波利斯</a>、圣保罗为上游，长约1010公里。地势低平，水流缓慢，河流两侧冰川湖泊、沼泽星罗棋布，湖水往往形成急流、瀑布，后注入干流。近明尼阿波利斯处，流经1.2公里长的峡谷急流带，落差19.5米，形成圣安东尼瀑布（落差5.4米）。</li>
<li>明尼阿波利斯、圣保罗至俄亥俄河口的开罗为中游，长约1373公里。圣路易斯以北河段，河床坡度大，两岸为悬崖峭壁，多急流险滩。<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%A3%E8%B7%AF%E6%98%93%E6%96%AF_(%E5%AF%86%E8%8B%8F%E9%87%8C%E5%B7%9E)" title="圣路易斯 (密苏里州)">圣路易斯</a>附近谷地开展，宽10～15公里。圣路易斯以南，河床比降减小，自开普吉拉多角以下，河流弯曲度明显增大，河谷逐渐变宽，俄亥俄河汇入处河宽达2.4公里。</li>
<li>开罗以下为下游，长约1567公里。流经平原地区，河宽一般为730～1370米，比降小，水流缓慢，多曲流、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%9B%E8%BB%9B%E6%B9%96" title="牛轭湖">牛轭湖</a>和沙洲，具有老年河特征。</li></ul>
<p>上游的春季融雪、雨水补给，4月为最高水位，6月降水增多，为次高水位，12月为低水位。中游的<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%86%E8%8B%8F%E9%87%8C%E6%B2%B3" title="密苏里河">密苏里河</a>注入，流量增至5800立方米/秒，最高水位在6月。下游的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%84%E4%BA%A5%E4%BF%84%E6%B2%B3" title="俄亥俄河">俄亥俄河</a>提供干流57％的水量，流量增至1.34万立方米/秒，4月为最高水位，10月为最低水位。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E8.88.AA.E8.BF.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="航运">航运</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：航运">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>密西西比河航运价值很大。1811年，“<a href="/wiki/%E6%96%B0%E5%A5%A5%E5%B0%94%E8%89%AF" title="新奥尔良">新奥尔良</a>”号汽轮首航密西西比河。当前年运输量在2亿吨以上。
</p><p>除了主流外，可通航的支流约有40条，水深2.75米的航道达1万公里，并通过运河与五大湖连成一巨大的内河航运系统。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.B2.BF.E5.B2.B8.E5.9F.8E.E5.B8.82"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="沿岸城市">沿岸城市</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：沿岸城市">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Missrivermpls.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="640" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Missrivermpls.jpg/220px-Missrivermpls.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Missrivermpls.jpg/330px-Missrivermpls.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Missrivermpls.jpg/440px-Missrivermpls.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Missrivermpls.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>密西西比河穿越明尼苏达州的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%98%8E%E5%B0%BC%E4%BA%9E%E6%B3%A2%E5%88%A9%E6%96%AF" title="明尼亚波利斯">明尼亚波利斯</a>（2007）</div></div></div>

<h2><span id=".E5.88.A5.E5.90.8D"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="别名">别名</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：别名">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>由于密西西比河的壮阔浩瀚及其历史意义，有许多别称：
</p>
<ul><li>父亲河（The Father of Waters）</li>
<li>The Gathering of Waters</li>
<li>The Big Muddy（更通常指密苏里河）</li>
<li>大河（Big River）</li>
<li>老人河（Old Man River）</li>
<li>伟大之河（The Great River）</li>
<li>国家之体（Body of a Nation）</li>
<li>The Mighty Mississippi</li>
<li>El Grande（de Soto）</li>
<li>The Muddy Mississippi</li>
<li>老蓝（Old Blue）</li>
<li>月河（Moon River）</li>
<li>密士失必河</li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E5.A8.B1.E4.B9.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="娱乐">娱乐</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：娱乐">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:MississippiRiverBluffs.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1748" data-file-width="1178" decoding="async" height="252" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/MississippiRiverBluffs.jpg/170px-MississippiRiverBluffs.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/MississippiRiverBluffs.jpg/255px-MississippiRiverBluffs.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/MississippiRiverBluffs.jpg/340px-MississippiRiverBluffs.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:MississippiRiverBluffs.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>威斯康辛靠近<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Lake Pepin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="丕平湖"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%95%E5%B9%B3%E6%B9%96&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="丕平湖（页面不存在）">丕平湖</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lake_Pepin" title="en:Lake Pepin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Lake Pepin</span></a></span>）</span></span>的一段<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Great River Road" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="大河之路"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%A7%E6%B2%B3%E4%B9%8B%E8%B7%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="大河之路（页面不存在）">大河之路</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_River_Road" title="en:Great River Road"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Great River Road</span></a></span>）</span></span>（2005）</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E6%BB%91%E6%B0%B4" title="滑水">滑水</a>被发明于威斯康辛和明尼苏达之间的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Lake Pepin" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="丕平湖"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B8%95%E5%B9%B3%E6%B9%96&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="丕平湖（页面不存在）">丕平湖</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lake_Pepin" title="en:Lake Pepin"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Lake Pepin</span></a></span>）</span></span>地区。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-usaws_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-usaws-8">[8]</a></sup><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Ralph Samuelson" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="拉尔夫·萨缪尔森"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%8B%89%E5%B0%94%E5%A4%AB%C2%B7%E8%90%A8%E7%BC%AA%E5%B0%94%E6%A3%AE&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="拉尔夫·萨缪尔森（页面不存在）">拉尔夫·萨缪尔森</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ralph_Samuelson" title="en:Ralph Samuelson"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Ralph Samuelson</span></a></span>）</span></span>在1922年发明并改进了他的滑水技术，并在1925年第一次表演了滑水跳跃。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-usaws_8-1"><a href="#cite_note-usaws-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p><p>沿着密西西比河有7个由<a href="/wiki/%E7%BE%8E%E5%9B%BD%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E5%85%AC%E5%9B%AD%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E5%B1%80" title="美国国家公园管理局">美国国家公园管理局</a>管理的区域。<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Mississippi National River and Recreation Area" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="密西西比河国家河流和娱乐区"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%B2%B3%E6%B5%81%E5%92%8C%E5%A8%B1%E4%B9%90%E5%8C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="密西西比河国家河流和娱乐区（页面不存在）">密西西比河国家河流和娱乐区</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mississippi_National_River_and_Recreation_Area" title="en:Mississippi National River and Recreation Area"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Mississippi National River and Recreation Area</span></a></span>）</span></span>是为了保护和展现密西西比河本身。其他6个区域是（按从北到南排列）：
</p>
<ul><li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Effigy Mounds National Monument" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="雕像古冢国家保护区"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%95%E5%83%8F%E5%8F%A4%E5%86%A2%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E5%8C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="雕像古冢国家保护区（页面不存在）">雕像古冢国家保护区</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Effigy_Mounds_National_Monument" title="en:Effigy Mounds National Monument"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Effigy Mounds National Monument</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9D%B0%E5%BC%97%E9%80%8A%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%89%A9%E5%BC%A0%E7%BA%AA%E5%BF%B5%E5%85%AC%E5%9B%AD" title="杰弗逊国家扩张纪念公园">杰弗逊国土扩张纪念碑</a>（<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Jefferson National Expansion Memorial" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="Jefferson National Expansion Memorial"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Jefferson_National_Expansion_Memorial&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Jefferson National Expansion Memorial（页面不存在）">Jefferson National Expansion Memorial</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jefferson_National_Expansion_Memorial" title="en:Jefferson National Expansion Memorial"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Jefferson National Expansion Memorial</span></a></span>）</span></span>）（简称：大拱门）</li>
<li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Vicksburg National Military Park" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="维克斯堡国家军事公园"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BB%B4%E5%85%8B%E6%96%AF%E5%A0%A1%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E5%86%9B%E4%BA%8B%E5%85%AC%E5%9B%AD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="维克斯堡国家军事公园（页面不存在）">维克斯堡国家军事公园</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vicksburg_National_Military_Park" title="en:Vicksburg National Military Park"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Vicksburg National Military Park</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
<li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Natchez National Historical Park" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="纳切兹国家历史公园"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%B3%E5%88%87%E5%85%B9%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E5%8E%86%E5%8F%B2%E5%85%AC%E5%9B%AD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="纳切兹国家历史公园（页面不存在）">纳切兹国家历史公园</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Natchez_National_Historical_Park" title="en:Natchez National Historical Park"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Natchez National Historical Park</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
<li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="New Orleans Jazz National Historical Park" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="新奥尔良爵士国家历史公园"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%96%B0%E5%A5%A5%E5%B0%94%E8%89%AF%E7%88%B5%E5%A3%AB%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E5%8E%86%E5%8F%B2%E5%85%AC%E5%9B%AD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="新奥尔良爵士国家历史公园（页面不存在）">新奥尔良爵士国家历史公园</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Orleans_Jazz_National_Historical_Park" title="en:New Orleans Jazz National Historical Park"><span dir="auto" lang="en">New Orleans Jazz National Historical Park</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
<li><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Jean Lafitte National Historical Park and Preserve" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="吉恩·拉菲特国家历史公园和保留地"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%90%89%E6%81%A9%C2%B7%E6%8B%89%E8%8F%B2%E7%89%B9%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E5%8E%86%E5%8F%B2%E5%85%AC%E5%9B%AD%E5%92%8C%E4%BF%9D%E7%95%99%E5%9C%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="吉恩·拉菲特国家历史公园和保留地（页面不存在）">吉恩·拉菲特国家历史公园和保留地</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jean_Lafitte_National_Historical_Park_and_Preserve" title="en:Jean Lafitte National Historical Park and Preserve"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Jean Lafitte National Historical Park and Preserve</span></a></span>）</span></span></li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E6.96.87.E5.8C.96.E5.BD.B1.E5.93.8D"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="文化影响">文化影响</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：文化影响">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E6.96.87.E5.AD.A6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="文学">文学</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：文学">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E5%A8%81%E5%BB%89%C2%B7%E7%A6%8F%E5%85%8B%E7%B4%8D" title="威廉·福克纳">威廉·福克纳</a>的大多数作品背景设定为他的故乡密西西比河流域与三角洲地区，并虚构了一个密西西比河流域的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8E%BF_(%E7%BE%8E%E5%9B%BD)" title="县 (美国)">县份</a><a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%A6%E5%85%8B%E7%BA%B3%E5%B8%95%E5%A1%94%E6%B3%95" title="约克纳帕塔法">约克纳帕塔法</a>。</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E9%A9%AC%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E5%90%90%E6%B8%A9" title="马克·吐温">马克·吐温</a>的许多作品的背景都是密西西比河，比如《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Life on the Mississippi" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="密西西比河上的生活"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3%E4%B8%8A%E7%9A%84%E7%94%9F%E6%B4%BB&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="密西西比河上的生活（页面不存在）">密西西比河上的生活</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Life_on_the_Mississippi" title="en:Life on the Mississippi"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Life on the Mississippi</span></a></span>）</span></span>》、《<a href="/wiki/%E6%B1%A4%E5%A7%86%C2%B7%E7%B4%A2%E4%BA%9A%E5%8E%86%E9%99%A9%E8%AE%B0" title="汤姆·索亚历险记">汤姆·索亚历险记</a>》、《<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%93%88%E5%85%8B%E8%B4%9D%E5%88%A9%C2%B7%E8%B4%B9%E6%81%A9%E5%8E%86%E9%99%A9%E8%AE%B0" title="哈克贝利·费恩历险记">哈克贝利·费恩历险记</a>》。</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E8%B5%AB%E5%B0%94%E6%9B%BC%C2%B7%E6%A2%85%E5%B0%94%E7%BB%B4%E5%B0%94" title="赫尔曼·梅尔维尔">赫尔曼·梅尔维尔</a>的小说《<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="The Confidence-Man" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="骗子 (小说)"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%AA%97%E5%AD%90_(%E5%B0%8F%E8%AF%B4)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="骗子 (小说)（页面不存在）">骗子</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Confidence-Man" title="en:The Confidence-Man"><span dir="auto" lang="en">The Confidence-Man</span></a></span>）</span></span>》（1857）讲述了一艘密西西比河的汽轮上的旅客们讲述的发生在密西西比河的故事。</li></ul>
<h3><span id=".E9.9F.B3.E4.B9.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="音乐">音乐</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：音乐">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h2><span id=".E7.9B.B8.E9.97.9C.E6.9D.A1.E7.9B.AE"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="相关条目">相关条目</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：相关条目">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.80.83.E6.96.87.E7.8D.BB"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参考文献">参考文献</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%86%E8%A5%BF%E8%A5%BF%E6%AF%94%E6%B2%B3&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：参考文献">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">美国地质调查局承认对于<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="River source" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="河流源头"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B2%B3%E6%B5%81%E6%BA%90%E5%A4%B4&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="河流源头（页面不存在）">河流源头</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/River_source" title="en:River source"><span dir="auto" lang="en">River source</span></a></span>）</span></span>有两个差别颇大的定义（<a class="external text" href="http://pubs.usgs.gov/of/1987/ofr87-242/" rel="nofollow">USGS.gov</a> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20170129040848/http://pubs.usgs.gov/of/1987/ofr87-242/" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>））。根据较严格的定义，密西西比河应该和它最长的支流——<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%86%E8%8B%8F%E9%87%8C%E6%B2%B3" title="密苏里河">密苏里河</a>共享同一源头，都在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%98%8E%E5%B0%BC%E8%8B%8F%E8%BE%BE%E5%B7%9E" title="明尼苏达州">明尼苏达州</a>的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Brower's Spring" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="布劳尔溪"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B8%83%E5%8A%B3%E5%B0%94%E6%BA%AA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="布劳尔溪（页面不存在）">布劳尔溪</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brower%27s_Spring" title="en:Brower's Spring"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Brower's Spring</span></a></span>）</span></span>。另外一个源头的定义承认其“结论有些随意”，认定源头在艾塔斯卡湖，并被广泛地接受。即使是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Jacob V. Brower" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="雅各布·范登堡·布劳尔"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9B%85%E5%90%84%E5%B8%83%C2%B7%E8%8C%83%E7%99%BB%E5%A0%A1%C2%B7%E5%B8%83%E5%8A%B3%E5%B0%94&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="雅各布·范登堡·布劳尔（页面不存在）">雅各布·范登堡·布劳尔</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jacob_V._Brower" title="en:Jacob V.
